### Agate — Full Correspondences
Core
- Essence: Survival, grounding, primal fear, endurance
- Element: Earth
- Colors: Red · Black · Brown
- Frequencies: 396 Hz · 228 Hz
- Note: C
- Geometry / Symbolism: Square · Four-petaled lotus
- Platonic Solids: Cube
- Physiology: Feet · Legs · Bones · Adrenals
- Chakras: Root

Astrological / Planetary
- Planets: Saturn · Mars
- Zodiac: Capricorn · Aries
- Kabbalah: Malkuth · Yesod
- Hebrew Letters: Tau · Peh
- Tarot: XXI The World · XVI The Tower

Cross-System
- Runes: Isa · Nauthiz · Uruz
- I Ching: ☷ K’un (Earth)
- Geomancy: Populus · Tristitia
- Minor Arcana: Pentacles (material foundation)
- Magical Tool: Pantacle · Stone
- Mayan Echo: Caban (Earth — movement)
- Numbers: 4

Alchemical
- Processes: Calcination · Coagulation
- Metals: Lead · Iron
- Crystals: Agate
- Plants: Oak · Patchouli
- Deities/Angels: Ganesha · Gaia · Michael

❤️ Flowing
Root is the bedrock, the earth’s embrace — anchoring the soul into form.

### Amethyst — Full Correspondences
Core
- Essence: Insight, intuition, inner vision
- Element: Light/Aether
- Colors: Indigo · Violet
- Frequencies: 852 Hz
- Note: A
- Geometry / Symbolism: Vesica within circle · Two-petaled lotus
- Platonic Solids: Dodecahedron (aether)
- Physiology: Pineal · Eyes · Forebrain
- Chakras: Third Eye · Crown

Astrological / Planetary
- Planets: Jupiter · Neptune
- Zodiac: Aquarius · Pisces
- Kabbalah: Chokmah · Binah
- Hebrew Letters: Tzaddi · Qoph
- Tarot: XVII The Star · XVIII The Moon

Cross-System
- Runes: Algiz · Ansuz
- I Ching: ☶ Gèn (Mountain)
- Geomancy: Acquisitio · Caput Draconis
- Minor Arcana: Swords (clarity, mind)
- Magical Tool: Mirror · Lamp
- Mayan Echo: Men (Eagle)
- Numbers: 7

Alchemical
- Processes: Sublimation · Fermentation
- Metals: Silver · —
- Crystals: Amethyst
- Plants: Mugwort · Blue Lotus
- Deities/Angels: Athena · Odin

❤️ Flowing
Third Eye is the inner horizon—pattern recognition in the dark.

### Aquamarine — Full Correspondences
Core
- Essence: Flow, desire, creativity, sensuality
- Element: Water
- Colors: Orange · Coral
- Frequencies: 417 Hz
- Note: D
- Geometry / Symbolism: Crescent · Six-petaled lotus
- Platonic Solids: Icosahedron
- Physiology: Reproductive organs · Kidneys · Fluids
- Chakras: Sacral · Throat

Astrological / Planetary
- Planets: Moon · Venus
- Zodiac: Cancer · Scorpio
- Kabbalah: Yesod · Netzach
- Hebrew Letters: Gimel · Nun
- Tarot: II The High Priestess · XIII Death

Cross-System
- Runes: Laguz · Perthro
- I Ching: ☵ Kǎn (Water)
- Geomancy: Via · Amissio
- Minor Arcana: Cups (emotion, flow)
- Magical Tool: Cup · Vessel
- Mayan Echo: Muluk (Offering/Water)
- Numbers: 2

Alchemical
- Processes: Dissolution · Separation
- Metals: Silver · Copper
- Crystals: Aquamarine
- Plants: Jasmine · Ylang-ylang
- Deities/Angels: Aphrodite · Oshun · Yemaya

❤️ Flowing
Sacral is the river—pleasure, creation, and the moon’s pull in the blood.

# 9. Alchemical Processes


### 1. Calcination
- Element: Fire
- Planets: Mars · Saturn
- Tarot: XVI The Tower
- Chakra: Root · Solar Plexus
- Metal: Lead · Iron
- Runes: Thurisaz (shock) · Isa (stillness)
- Crystals: Obsidian · Garnet
- Virtues: Purification · Awakening
- Vices: Destruction · Harshness
- Deities: Ares · Sekhmet · Hades
- Magical Tools: Furnace · Athanor
- Mayan Echo: Cimi (death, transformation)
- Gloss: Burning away the false; destruction that reveals essence.
- Cross-References: Mars/Saturn → Tower → Root/Solar Plexus → Thurisaz/Isa

---

### 2. Dissolution
- Element: Water
- Planets: Moon · Neptune
- Tarot: II The High Priestess · XVIII The Moon
- Chakra: Sacral
- Metal: Silver
- Runes: Laguz (flow) · Perthro (mystery)
- Crystals: Pearl · Moonstone
- Virtues: Release · Intuition
- Vices: Loss of form · Confusion
- Deities: Isis · Yemaya · Chandra
- Magical Tools: Cauldron · Chalice
- Mayan Echo: Muluc (water, offering)
- Gloss: Ego dissolves into the waters of psyche; preparation for transformation.
- Cross-References: Moon/Neptune → Priestess/Moon → Sacral → Laguz/Perthro

---

### 3. Separation
- Element: Air
- Planet: Mercury
- Tarot: I The Magician · XI Justice
- Chakra: Throat
- Metal: Mercury
- Runes: Ansuz (articulation) · Gebo (discernment)
- Crystals: Lapis Lazuli · Agate
- Virtues: Discernment · Clarity
- Vices: Division · Cold intellect
- Deities: Thoth · Hermes · Athena
- Magical Tools: Sword · Scalpel
- Mayan Echo: Ik (wind, communication)
- Gloss: Distilling the pure from the impure, mind’s scalpel separating truth.
- Cross-References: Mercury → Magician/Justice → Throat → Ansuz/Gebo

---

### 4. Conjunction
- Element: Earth
- Planets: Venus · Jupiter
- Tarot: VI Lovers · III The Empress
- Chakra: Heart
- Metal: Copper · Tin
- Runes: Gebo (gift) · Wunjo (harmony)
- Crystals: Rose Quartz · Emerald
- Virtues: Union · Fertility
- Vices: Attachment · Indulgence
- Deities: Aphrodite · Isis · Osiris
- Magical Tools: Wedding Cup · Altar
- Mayan Echo: Oc (dog, union, loyalty)
- Gloss: Marriage of opposites, hieros gamos; balancing forces in love.
- Cross-References: Venus/Jupiter → Lovers/Empress → Heart → Gebo/Wunjo

---

### 5. Fermentation
- Element: Air/Spirit
- Planets: Uranus · Pluto
- Tarot: XIII Death · XX Judgment
- Chakra: Ajna
- Metals: Uranium · Plutonium
- Runes: Eihwaz (axis) · Dagaz (breakthrough)
- Crystals: Moldavite · Amethyst
- Virtues: Inspiration · Renewal
- Vices: Madness · Obsession
- Deities: Dionysus · Shiva · Osiris
- Magical Tools: Alembic · Sacred Wine
- Mayan Echo: K’an (seed, new growth)
- Gloss: Putrefaction and spirit’s spark; fermentation births new life.
- Cross-References: Uranus/Pluto → Death/Judgment → Ajna → Eihwaz/Dagaz

---

### 6. Distillation
- Element: Fire/Aether
- Planet: Sun
- Tarot: XIX The Sun
- Chakra: Crown
- Metal: Gold
- Runes: Sowilo (victory) · Kenaz (flame)
- Crystals: Citrine · Diamond

- Vices: Pride · Over-refinement

- Magical Tools: Alembic · Distiller

- Gloss: Essence rises in vapor; clarity shines as distilled light.
- Cross-References: Sun → The Sun → Crown → Sowilo/Kenaz

---

### 7. Coagulation

---

### 8. Sublimation

⚪ 1 — Monad (Unity) — Full Correspondences

Core
- Essence: Source, singularity, origin of all forms  
- Element: Aether / Spirit  
- Colors: White · Gold · Clear  
- Frequencies: 432 Hz · 963 Hz  
- Note: C♯ / B (higher octave)  
- Geometry: Point · Circle · Sphere  
- Physiology: Crown · Pineal seed · Breath of origin  

Astrological / Planetary
- Planets: Sun (core vitality) · Uranus (awakening)  
- Zodiac: Leo (solar heart) · Aquarius (cosmic current)  
- Kabbalah: Kether (Crown)  
- Hebrew Letters: Aleph א (breath, ox, primordial air)  
- Tarot: 0 The Fool (seed potential) · XIX The Sun (singularity revealed)  

Cross-System
- Runes: Isa (ice, stillness) · Ansuz (breath of spirit)  
- I Ching: ☰ Qian (Heaven, pure yang)  
- Geomancy: Via (path, beginning)  
- Minor Arcana: Aces (pure potential in each suit)  
- Magical Tool: Wand as staff · Crown · Circle  
- Mayan Echo: Ahau (Sun — enlightenment, radiant source)  
- Numbers: 1  

Alchemical
- Processes: Sublimation (essence rising) · Projection (seed into form)  
- Metals: Gold (unity) · Quicksilver (primordial movement)  
- Crystals: Diamond · Clear Quartz · Opal  
- Plants: Lotus · Frankincense  
- Deities/Angels: Ra · Helios · Brahma · Metatron  

Rational Anchor
One point defines existence itself. The Monad is rationally true as the seed of all mathematics and geometry — the origin from which all multiplicity emerges.

✨ Flowing
Monad is the point before all division — the radiant seed, the single flame from which the ten thousand things unfold.

- Deities/Angels: Hermes · Prometheus · Durga  

Rational Anchor
The octagon mediates between circle and square. Rationally, the Ogdoad represents **transition and infinity**, bridging heaven and earth.  

🕗 Flowing  
Ogdoad is the threshold of infinity — the eternal cycle, the balanced loop of renewal.


---

🔹 9 — Ennead (Completion / Gestation) — Full Correspondences

Core
- Essence: Gestation, fulfillment, completion of cycles  
- Element: Water · Fire · Spirit  
- Colors: Purple · Gold · Black  
- Frequencies: 432 Hz · 528 Hz  
- Note: F  
- Geometry: Enneagon · Enneagram · Triple Triad  
- Physiology: Nine-month human gestation · Nine openings of the body  

Astrological / Planetary
- Planets: Mars (struggle) · Jupiter (expansion)  
- Zodiac: Sagittarius (vision) · Aries (birth)  
- Kabbalah: Yesod (foundation)  
- Hebrew Letters: Teth ט (serpent of gestation)  
- Tarot: IX The Hermit · IX of Cups (fulfillment)  

Cross-System
- Runes: Jera (harvest cycle) · Sowilo (completion)  
- I Ching: 9 as return before completion  
- Geomancy: Populus (many, full)  
- Minor Arcana: Nines (completion, fullness)  
- Magical Tool: Lantern (Hermit’s lamp)  
- Mayan Echo: Bolon (Nine Lords of the Night)  
- Numbers: 9  

Alchemical
- Processes: Fermentation (gestation) · Distillation (refinement)  
- Metals: Silver (Moon) · Tin (Jupiter)  
- Crystals: Amethyst · Topaz · Sapphire  
- Plants: Wheat · Grapevine  
- Deities/Angels: Isis (nine months) · Odin (nine nights on Yggdrasil)  

Rational Anchor
Nine is three triads, and 9 returns to 1 in digital root. Rationally, the Ennead is **gestation and cyclic completion**.  

🔹 Flowing  
Ennead is the womb of completion — the ninefold circle, the fullness before rebirth.

🔟 10 — Decad (Cosmos / Tetractys) — Full Correspondences

Core
- Essence: Wholeness, manifestation, cosmic order  
- Element: All elements united  
- Colors: White · Gold · Rainbow spectrum  
- Frequencies: 432 Hz · 963 Hz  
- Note: C major chord (1 + 3 + 5 + octave)  
- Geometry: Tetractys (1+2+3+4=10) · Decagon · Decagram  
- Physiology: Completion of cycles · Full body integration  

Astrological / Planetary
- Planets: Sun (center of cycle) · Saturn (completion)  
- Zodiac: Capricorn (cosmic law) · Leo (cosmic radiance)  
- Kabbalah: Malkuth (Kingdom, 10th sephira)  
- Hebrew Letters: Yod י (seed of creation)  
- Tarot: X Wheel of Fortune · X of Pentacles  

Cross-System
- Runes: Dagaz (new cycle) · Fehu (abundance manifest)  
- I Ching: 10 — Conduct, treading the path  
- Geomancy: Caput Draconis (new cycle)  
- Minor Arcana: Tens (completion, legacy)  
- Magical Tool: Circle · Decagram  
- Mayan Echo: Lahun (completion of cycles)  
- Numbers: 10  

Alchemical
- Processes: Rubedo (redness, final integration) · Coagulation (stone complete)  
- Metals: Gold (perfection) · Lead (resolved)  
- Crystals: Diamond · Clear Quartz · Ruby  
- Plants: Oak (wholeness) · Rose (tenfold petals)  
- Deities/Angels: Pythagoras (tetractys) · Metatron · Sophia  

Rational Anchor
The Tetractys shows 1+2+3+4=10. Rationally, the Decad is the **manifest cosmos** — the return to unity after the cycle of multiplicity.  

🔟 Flowing  
Decad is the whole circle of being — the cosmic return, the universe breathing as One.
